## üîç Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### üéØ Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 37 page(s) - 380 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R74: No description](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)
**Issue**: The font size is specified using an absolute unit

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<p>...</p>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/p
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/p')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:

**Rule**: [list](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/list?application=playwright)

**HTML Pattern**:

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://nexxt.com.au/

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="/contact" class="theme-btn">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="theme-btn"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/nexxtgroup/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/" class="logo">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="logo"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/contact" class="theme-btn">Contact Us</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="theme-btn"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/contact" class="theme-btn2">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="theme-btn2"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/transformation-and-change">Transformation & Change</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="nav-link active" id="development-tab" data-bs-toggle="tab" href="#development" role="tab" aria-controls="development" aria-selected="true">Queensland Government</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="development-tab"]`

*... and 5 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R113](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r113)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<span class="swiper-pagination-bullet swiper-pagination-bullet-active" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Go to slide 1" aria-current="true" />`
- XPath: `/span[@class="swiper-pagination-bullet swiper-pagination-bullet-active"]`

- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1">Op Ed</h6>`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `banner` have the same name.

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.1:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

- XPath: `/ul`

- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle">INSIGHTS</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1">Op Ed</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Contact Info</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `banner` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.1:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R68: Accessible name contains the visible label text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r68)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element owns no elements as required by its semantic role
- HTML: `<ul />`
- XPath: `/ul`

#### Rule: [SIA-R69: Text has sufficient contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r69)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.1:1 which is         below the required contrast of 4.5:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>Our team shares stories and lessons from working w...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle badge-radius">Our Studies</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle badge-radius"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle">INSIGHTS</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle"]`

- HTML: `<a href="/agile-20-years-on">Agile 20 years on...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm" href="/insights-inner">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="elementor-button elementor-button-link elementor-size-sm"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button id="submit2" class="theme-btn">Subscribe</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="submit2"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="https://nexxt.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/NEXXT-250-scaled.jpg" />`
- XPath: `/img`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle">INSIGHTS</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1">Op Ed</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Contact Info</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `banner` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.1:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

- XPath: `/ul`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>Our team shares stories and lessons from working w...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next

- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle badge-radius"]`

- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="next page-numbers" href="https://nexxt.com.au/author/mnitish0gmail-com/page/2/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="next page-numbers"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/nexxtgroup/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/" class="logo">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="logo"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/contact" class="theme-btn">Contact Us</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="theme-btn"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://nexxt.com.au/">Home</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button id="submit2" class="theme-btn">Subscribe</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="submit2"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>Services</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `banner` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R62: Links are visually distinguishable from surrounding text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r62)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link is not distinguishable from the surrounding text
- HTML: `<a href="https://nexxt.com.au/category/blog/">Blog</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.1:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R68: Accessible name contains the visible label text](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r68)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element owns no elements as required by its semantic role
- HTML: `<ul />`
- XPath: `/ul`

#### Rule: [SIA-R69: Text has sufficient contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r69)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 3.1:1 which is         below the required contrast of 4.5:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="meta">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="meta"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="meta">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="meta"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R80: ASCII art has a text alternative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r80)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>If you‚Äôre spinning up initiatives without clear ou...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R83: Text can be resized to 200% without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r83)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is clipped

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<span class="swiper-pagination-bullet swiper-pagination-bullet-active" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Go to slide 1" aria-current="true" />`
- XPath: `/span[@class="swiper-pagination-bullet swiper-pagination-bullet-active"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<span class="swiper-pagination-bullet" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Go to slide 2" />`
- XPath: `/span[@class="swiper-pagination-bullet"]`

- Message: The image does not have an accessible name

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name

- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<span class="swiper-pagination-bullet swiper-pagination-bullet-active" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Go to slide 1" aria-current="true" />`
- XPath: `/span[@class="swiper-pagination-bullet swiper-pagination-bullet-active"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size and spacing
- HTML: `<span class="swiper-pagination-bullet" tabindex="0" role="button" aria-label="Go to slide 2" />`
- XPath: `/span[@class="swiper-pagination-bullet"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img decoding="async" class="desktop fade-in" src="https://nexxt.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/NEXXT-226-1-scaled.jpg" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="desktop fade-in"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img decoding="async" src="https://nexxt.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/Badge.jpeg" style="touch-action: pan-y;" />`
- XPath: `/img`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img decoding="async" src="https://nexxt.com.au/wp-content/uploads/2024/11/big-data2.png" class="service-icon" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="service-icon"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R53: Headings follow a logical hierarchy](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h4>...</h4>`
- XPath: `/h4`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1">Op Ed</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The heading skips one or more levels
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle">Tips</h6>`
- XPath: `/h6[@class="section-subtitle"]`

- Message: Some `banner` have the same name.

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://nexxt.com.au/

#### Rule: [color-contrast](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/color-contrast?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<a href="/contact" class="theme-btn">Contact Us</a>`
- XPath: `.header-left-right > .theme-btn[href$="contact"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<a href="/about-us" class="theme-btn">Learn More</a>`
- XPath: `.theme-btn[href$="about-us"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p>                             Years  <span>of Customer <br>Success</span>                        </p>`
- XPath: `.experience-content > p`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<p>                         50+  <span>Years of combined business and digital expertise</span>                    </p>`
- XPath: `.our-expert-team-box-inner > p`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Elements must meet minimum color contrast ratio thresholds
- HTML: `<span class="section-subtitle">CASE STUDIES</span>`
- XPath: `.case-studio-header > p > .section-subtitle`

*... and 11 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4><a href="/transformation-and-change">Transformation &amp; Change</a></h4>`
- XPath: `.service-card.simple-shadow:nth-child(1) > h4`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>Accelerating Delivery, Inspiring Change</h4>`
- XPath: `#development > .case-studio-body.d-flex > .right > .case-studio-contents.service-card.card-h > h4`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>Assess</h4>`
- XPath: `.about-timeline-item:nth-child(1) > .about-timeline-item-inner > h4`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle section-subtitle1">Op Ed</h6>`
- XPath: `.section-subtitle1`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h6 class="section-subtitle">Tips</h6>`
- XPath: `.news-item.card-h:nth-child(1) > .news-item-body > h6`

*... and 4 more failures for this rule*

- XPath: `.imgs > img[decoding="async"]`
